  <script>
   wbq.push(function manageHamburgerMenu() {
  var $nav = $('.js__nav');
  var $navCloseBtn = $('#nav-close-btn');
  var $navToggleBtn = $('.js__btn--nav-toggle');

  function lockNavFocus() {
    $navCloseBtn.focus();
    document.addEventListener('focusin', focusNavCloseBtn);
  }

  function focusNavCloseBtn(event) {
    if (!$.contains(document.getElementById('masthead-nav'), event.target)) {
      $navCloseBtn.focus();
    }
  }

  function unlockNavFocus() {
    document.removeEventListener('focusin', focusNavCloseBtn);
    $navToggleBtn.focus();
  }

  // hamburger menu to toggle mobile nav, full screen hit area beneath
  // mobile nav to act as toggle target
  $navToggleBtn.click(function (event) {
    $nav.toggleClass('nav--is-open');
    if ($nav.hasClass('nav--is-open')) {
      if (window.DEVICE_VIEW === 'desktop') {
        lockNavFocus();
      }
      window.TMZ.utils.setAccessibilityFocusTrap('masthead-nav');
      $nav.css('visibility', 'visible');
    } else {
      window.TMZ.utils.removeAccessibilityFocusTrap();
      if (window.DEVICE_VIEW === 'desktop') {
        unlockNavFocus();
        $navToggleBtn.focus();
      }
      setTimeout(function () {
        $nav.css('visibility', 'hidden');
      }, 300);
    }

    event.preventDefault();
  });
});
  </script>
  <!--/.nav-->

  <script>
   wbq.push(function manageTipMenu() {
  var $tip = $('.js__tip');
  var $tipCloseBtn = $('#tip__btn-close');
  var $tipToggleBtn = $('.js__btn--tip-toggle');
  var $nav = $('.js__nav');

  function lockTipFocus() {
    $tipCloseBtn.focus();
    document.addEventListener('focusin', focusTipCloseBtn);
  }

  function focusTipCloseBtn(event) {
    if (!$.contains(document.getElementById('tip'), event.target)) {
      $tipCloseBtn.focus();
    }
  }

  function unlockTipFocus() {
    document.removeEventListener('focusin', focusTipCloseBtn);
  }

  // toggle tip full screen mobile menu
  $tipToggleBtn.click(function (event) {
    $tip.toggleClass('tip--is-open');
    if ($tip.hasClass('tip--is-open')) {
      if (window.DEVICE_VIEW === 'desktop') {
        lockTipFocus();
      }
      window.TMZ.utils.setAccessibilityFocusTrap('tip');
      $tip.css('visibility', 'visible');
      setTimeout(function() {
        $nav.css('visibility', 'hidden');
      }, 300);
    } else {
      window.TMZ.utils.removeAccessibilityFocusTrap();
      if (window.DEVICE_VIEW === 'desktop') {
        unlockTipFocus();
        $tipToggleBtn.focus();
      }
      setTimeout(function() {
        $tip.css('visibility', 'hidden');
      }, 300);
    }

    // Hide nav
    if ($nav.hasClass('nav--is-open')) {
      setTimeout(function () {
        $nav.removeClass('nav--is-open');
      }, 300);
    }
    event.preventDefault();
  });
});
  </script>

          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-55d69844-f156-40ec-a8f0-40c986fa8a20-515442214-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-55d69844-f156-40ec-a8f0-40c986fa8a20-515442214-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-55d69844-f156-40ec-a8f0-40c986fa8a20-515442214-footer');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-55d69844-f156-40ec-a8f0-40c986fa8a20-515442214-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-55d69844-f156-40ec-a8f0-40c986fa8a20-515442214-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-55d69844-f156-40ec-a8f0-40c986fa8a20-515442214-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-55d69844-f156-40ec-a8f0-40c986fa8a20-515442214-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-55d69844-f156-40ec-a8f0-40c986fa8a20-515442214'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-55d69844-f156-40ec-a8f0-40c986fa8a20-515442214-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-55d69844-f156-40ec-a8f0-40c986fa8a20-515442214-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-02-030221-dolly-parton-1049138/',
                  null,
                  'tmz:video:55d69844-f156-40ec-a8f0-40c986fa8a20',
                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }
      });

         </p>

         </p>
        </section>

         </p>

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-e679474371b23ba45b4d7777163f32e0">
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/joe-exotic/">
           <strong>
            Joe Exotic
           </strong>
          </a>
          is getting the best revenge he can against
          <strong>
           Carole Baskin
          </strong>
          -- hiring the attorney who recently repped the family of her missing husband ... who's now working to free him.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-e679474371b23ba45b4d7777163f32e0-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-46969881e2c2c82fc33c2861ad31f600">
         <p>
          <strong>
           John M. Phillips
          </strong>
          of the Phillips &amp; Hunt firm broke the news Tuesday, saying he'd been retained by the 'Tiger King' himself in a bid to get a new trial arranged so Joe can plead his case in front of a new set of 12 jurors.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-46969881e2c2c82fc33c2861ad31f600-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-678d4c6e50d709595b59db1214bb9daf">
         <p>
          Phillips writes, "Work has already begun on @joe_exotic's New Trial Motion. We are proud to be leading his team. I was sworn into the Western District of Oklahoma this morning. This isn't about tigers, television or tomfoolery, it's about justice and evidence. More soon."
         </p>
        </section>

                  "contentUrl": "https://ovp.tmz.com/video/4d/o/2021/03/02/4d05d9a7b5f34351a25f3a6845387805.mp4",
                          "embedUrl": "https://share.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-02-030221-john-phillips-1049151/",
                "author": {
          "@type": "Person",
          "name": "TMZ Staff"
        },
                "publisher": {
          "@type": "Organization",
          "name": "TMZ",
          "logo": {
            "@type": "ImageObject",
            "url": "https://static.tmz.com/tmz-web/img/tmz-logo-red-147x60-v1.png",
            "height": 60,
            "width": 147
          }
        }
      }
         </script>
         <script>
          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-9b3d2bce-9170-41b3-8a22-f715d92fce8b-1067125575-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-9b3d2bce-9170-41b3-8a22-f715d92fce8b-1067125575-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-9b3d2bce-9170-41b3-8a22-f715d92fce8b-1067125575-footer');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-9b3d2bce-9170-41b3-8a22-f715d92fce8b-1067125575-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-9b3d2bce-9170-41b3-8a22-f715d92fce8b-1067125575-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-9b3d2bce-9170-41b3-8a22-f715d92fce8b-1067125575-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-9b3d2bce-9170-41b3-8a22-f715d92fce8b-1067125575-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-9b3d2bce-9170-41b3-8a22-f715d92fce8b-1067125575'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-9b3d2bce-9170-41b3-8a22-f715d92fce8b-1067125575-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-9b3d2bce-9170-41b3-8a22-f715d92fce8b-1067125575-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-02-030221-john-phillips-1049151/',
                  null,
                  'tmz:video:9b3d2bce-9170-41b3-8a22-f715d92fce8b',
                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }
      });
         </script>
        </section>

         <p>
          He also posted a video ... which took some shots at Joe's former legal team, who Phillips characterized as engaging in "buffoonery" in their bid to get JE pardoned by Prez
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/donald-trump/">

           </strong>
          </a>

         <p>
          Doesn't sound like Joe disagrees -- at least that's how Phillips makes it sound. He says shortly after
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/01/20/president-trump-snubbed-pardon-joe-exotic-tiger-king/">
           <strong>
            the failed attempt
           </strong>
          </a>
          , the man himself reached out and asked about his services. One thing led to another, and now Phillips is on the case -- and he ain't looking to
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/joe-biden/">
           <strong>
            Joe Biden
           </strong>
          </a>
          for a bail-out either.

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-46995348351583139c22ae40bb57af96">
         <p>
          It's unclear how much cheddar Joel dropped for this pad ... but the penthouse's asking price was a cool $29.5 million. Pretty sure Joel can afford it ... he sold Grindr in 2008 for $245m.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-46995348351583139c22ae40bb57af96-->
       </div>
       <!--/.article__blocks-->

      <article class="article" id="blogroll-23e657f6-d130-4933-bdba-d8ad30b4a9a7">
       <div class="article__channel--viral">
       </div>
       <header class="article__header">
        <a class="article__header-link js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"headline","pos":5}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:23e657f6-d130-4933-bdba-d8ad30b4a9a7" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/02/dr-seuss-step-daughter-dont-pull-books-disclaimer/">
         <h2 class="article__header-title">
          <span class="article__hf1 text-uppercase h3">
           Dr. Seuss' Stepdaughter
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf2 text-none h2">
           Stop Hopping On My Pop ...
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf3 text-uppercase h1">
           Don't Pull Books, Add Disclaimer
          </span>
         </h2>
        </a>
        <h5 class="article__published-at">
         <ul class="social social--sm">
          <li class="social-item">
           <a aria-label="Share on Facebook" class="btn social__btn social__btn--sm social__btn--facebook js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"facebook-header","pos":5}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:23e657f6-d130-4933-bdba-d8ad30b4a9a7" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/02/dr-seuss-step-daughter-dont-pull-books-disclaimer/" onclick="window.open('http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tmz.com%2F2021%2F03%2F02%2Fdr-seuss-step-daughter-dont-pull-books-disclaimer%2F', '_blank', 'status=0,width=575,height=450');return false;">
            <span aria-label="Facebook" class="icon icon-facebook--white social__icon--facebook" role="img">
            </span>
            <span class="social__count">
             4.9K
            </span>
            <span class="sr-only">
             shares
            </span>
           </a>
          </li>
          <li class="social-item">
           <a aria-label="Share on Twitter" class="btn social__btn social__btn--sm social__btn--twitter js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"twitter-header","pos":5}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:23e657f6-d130-4933-bdba-d8ad30b4a9a7" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/02/dr-seuss-step-daughter-dont-pull-books-disclaimer/" onclick="window.open('https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tmz.com%2F2021%2F03%2F02%2Fdr-seuss-step-daughter-dont-pull-books-disclaimer%2F&amp;text=Dr.%20Seuss%27%20Stepdaughter%20Says%20Books%20Shouldn%27t%20Be%20Pulled&amp;via=TMZ&amp;related=HarveyLevinTMZ', '_blank', 'status=0,width=575,height=450');return false;">
            <span aria-label="Twitter" class="icon icon-sd icon-twitter--white" role="img">
            </span>
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <!--/.social-->
         3/2/2021 10:55 AM PT
        </h5>
        <!--/.article__posted-date-->
       </header>
       <div class="article__blocks">
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default canvas-block-is-first " id="cb-4afdb6c49f927110e1bc0aa3cb532037">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/6b/4by3/2021/03/02/6b8f34e20059400abcf218f27a07cd4b_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="media-swipe image-block__media-swipe">
           Exclusive
          </div>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            Getty/Vanguard Press/Random House
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-4afdb6c49f927110e1bc0aa3cb532037-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-b2d43eec7dbe523e21c470246531d55c">
         <p>
          <strong>
           Dr. Seuss
          </strong>
          ' books should NOT be yanked from shelves -- because all they need is a little context on page 1 ... so says a woman who was raised by the man himself.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-b2d43eec7dbe523e21c470246531d55c-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-ab72d58d43825235fd355ce3c174174b">
         <p>
          <strong>
           Leagrey Dimond
          </strong>
          -- one of Dr. Seuss' stepdaughters -- tells TMZ she doesn't think his work needs to be censored or stored away from public view ... which is essentially what Dr. Seuss Enterprises did on Monday.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-ab72d58d43825235fd355ce3c174174b-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-be4bbc7b08b4f197f9ad00f1d603bbc6">
         <p>
          Instead, Dimond suggests adding a disclaimer to the 6 books in question ... something a lot of media companies have been opting for lately for questionable or outdated material with racist depictions. The same thing should happen here, in Dimond's eyes anyway.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-be4bbc7b08b4f197f9ad00f1d603bbc6-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default " id="cb-dc57178bbc780a37a61969466d89e782">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/0f/4by3/2021/03/02/0f02384ac4a24198a06a52c64bc76deb_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            Shutterstock Premier
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-dc57178bbc780a37a61969466d89e782-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-11fdc16a9648a956100d1921dcfafba3">
         <p>
          She also has this to say about Seuss' work -- yes, some of his earlier publications and illustrations DID feature racist imagery, but his legacy shouldn't hinge on that alone ... as she insists the full breadth of his literature shows he's a good guy and evolved over time.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-11fdc16a9648a956100d1921dcfafba3-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-ec8faf89763d0799c0ec841ff84ec532">
         <p>
          Dimond says Seuss publicly regretted some of his earlier work -- such as ads, comic strips and political cartoons he helped craft during the WWII era -- which featured
          <a href="https://twitter.com/Isabella_Scar/status/1366801822942388228" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
           <strong>
            blatantly racist drawings
           </strong>
          </a>
          of Black people and Asian people.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-ec8faf89763d0799c0ec841ff84ec532-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-f89bbe17387fb3e2a1831edf1dbc95f4">
         <p>
          But, there's a bigger reason the org bearing his name should hold off, per LD ... nobody who runs the place knew him personally.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-f89bbe17387fb3e2a1831edf1dbc95f4-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-twitter-tweet-block canvas-twitter-tweet-block-blogroll canvas-twitter-tweet-block--default " id="cb-41279efaff2bc3a6026b32c7cd5a9987">
         <div class="d-flex justify-content-center" id="cb-41279efaff2bc3a6026b32c7cd5a9987-1033035248-target">
          <blockquote class="twitter-tweet">
           <p dir="ltr" lang="en">
            There are other Dr Seuss books that dont include such blatant racism... A chinaman who eats with sticks.
            <a href="https://t.co/EPMVRr5SJV">
             pic.twitter.com/EPMVRr5SJV
            </a>
           </p>
            Josh Leo (@joshleo)
           <a href="https://twitter.com/joshleo/status/1251510650469310464?ref_src=twsrc^tfw">
            April 18, 2020
           </a>
           <a href="https://twitter.com/joshleo" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
            @joshleo
           </a>
          </blockquote>
         </div>

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-e1e6023cfbc23bf0d91b9bb2a06da76d">
         <p>
          Dimond says since coming into Seuss' care at age 9, she never once experienced any hatred, hate speech or bigotry of any kind ... which she says was emblematic of his character at large. The fact people are judging him in death, she says, doesn't sit right with her.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-e1e6023cfbc23bf0d91b9bb2a06da76d-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-b575eb20a01a53e177b609b133f9ea93">
         <p>
          You'll recall -- the Enterprise announced it was
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/02/dr-seuss-books-racist-imagery-biden-print/">
           <strong>
            ceasing further sales
           </strong>
          </a>
          of 6 Seuss children's books -- including "And to Think That I Saw It on Mulberry Street," "Scrambled Eggs Super!" "If I Ran the Zoo," "McElligots Pool," "On Beyond Zebra!" and "The Cats Quizzer"
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-b575eb20a01a53e177b609b133f9ea93-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-twitter-tweet-block canvas-twitter-tweet-block-blogroll canvas-twitter-tweet-block--default " id="cb-05401a8fe7b50867f657f4db2418e9d7">

          </blockquote>

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-23d18b3d02a45d0930af002957c6281d">
         <p>
          Some examples of the problematic imagery -- from 'Mulberry' and 'Zoo' -- feature Asian stereotypes ... like referring to one character as a "Chinaman ... with sticks."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-23d18b3d02a45d0930af002957c6281d-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-bfff49421bd3eece7248800f76ba754b">
         <p>
          In any case, his stepdaughter thinks it's a shame he's being muzzled all these years later -- and on his birthday, no less.
         </p>
        </section>

         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/tamar-braxton/">
           <strong>
            Tamar Braxton
           </strong>
          </a>
          no longer has to keep her distance from her ex-boyfriend ... because weve learned his restraining order's been dissolved after neither one of them showed up in court.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-6e1958b26f1ca6db3ad2a9cfd8e5b6ee-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-50643d5b184b8d82aa3eb0cfd8d69c44">
         <p>
          Neither Tamar nor the singer's ex,
          <strong>
           David Adefeso
          </strong>
          , appeared for their court hearing on the matter Tuesday, so the judge dismissed the case and dissolved the restraining order.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-50643d5b184b8d82aa3eb0cfd8d69c44-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-41f2629a715883b0fb7d2b075eeb80b7">
         <p>
          We broke the story ... Adefeso filed for a
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2020/09/08/tamar-braxton-boyfriend-domestic-violence-restraining-order/">
           <strong>
            domestic violence restraining order
           </strong>
          </a>
          against Tamar in September and was temporarily granted one. David claimed Tamar attacked him while he was driving his car and threatened to have him killed.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-41f2629a715883b0fb7d2b075eeb80b7-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-1c636bbeb38c26acdba93259e1af07cc">
         <p>
          Tamar denied the allegations the following month on "The Tamron Hall Show."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-1c636bbeb38c26acdba93259e1af07cc-->

          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-7fa98376-0f25-5f1d-be29-55721b87fc02-1648421428-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-7fa98376-0f25-5f1d-be29-55721b87fc02-1648421428-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-7fa98376-0f25-5f1d-be29-55721b87fc02-1648421428-footer');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-7fa98376-0f25-5f1d-be29-55721b87fc02-1648421428-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-7fa98376-0f25-5f1d-be29-55721b87fc02-1648421428-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-7fa98376-0f25-5f1d-be29-55721b87fc02-1648421428-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-7fa98376-0f25-5f1d-be29-55721b87fc02-1648421428-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-7fa98376-0f25-5f1d-be29-55721b87fc02-1648421428'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-7fa98376-0f25-5f1d-be29-55721b87fc02-1648421428-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-7fa98376-0f25-5f1d-be29-55721b87fc02-1648421428-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/072020-tamar-braxton-911-v2-4821771-0-2plxdc6f/',

                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }
      });

         <script>
          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-9473adb5-2ae6-4858-baa9-26fc5b3fd766-780896651-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-9473adb5-2ae6-4858-baa9-26fc5b3fd766-780896651-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-9473adb5-2ae6-4858-baa9-26fc5b3fd766-780896651-footer');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-9473adb5-2ae6-4858-baa9-26fc5b3fd766-780896651-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-9473adb5-2ae6-4858-baa9-26fc5b3fd766-780896651-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-9473adb5-2ae6-4858-baa9-26fc5b3fd766-780896651-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-9473adb5-2ae6-4858-baa9-26fc5b3fd766-780896651-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-9473adb5-2ae6-4858-baa9-26fc5b3fd766-780896651'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-9473adb5-2ae6-4858-baa9-26fc5b3fd766-780896651-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-9473adb5-2ae6-4858-baa9-26fc5b3fd766-780896651-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-02-030221-jj-watt-1049019/',
                  null,

                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }

        "dateModified": "2021-03-02T08:20:08Z",
                "width": "560",
        "height": "315",
                  "contentUrl": "https://ovp.tmz.com/video/84/o/2021/03/01/84baedfad29b4332aac85c718f397bba.mp4",
                          "embedUrl": "https://share.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-01-030121-ellen-tullos-1048444/",
                "author": {
          "@type": "Person",
          "name": "TMZ Staff"
        },

         <script>
          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-2e5e28c6-cd9a-4fec-b8a2-1bdc14f86632-473188283-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-2e5e28c6-cd9a-4fec-b8a2-1bdc14f86632-473188283-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-2e5e28c6-cd9a-4fec-b8a2-1bdc14f86632-473188283-footer');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-2e5e28c6-cd9a-4fec-b8a2-1bdc14f86632-473188283-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-2e5e28c6-cd9a-4fec-b8a2-1bdc14f86632-473188283-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-2e5e28c6-cd9a-4fec-b8a2-1bdc14f86632-473188283-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-2e5e28c6-cd9a-4fec-b8a2-1bdc14f86632-473188283-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-2e5e28c6-cd9a-4fec-b8a2-1bdc14f86632-473188283'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-2e5e28c6-cd9a-4fec-b8a2-1bdc14f86632-473188283-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-2e5e28c6-cd9a-4fec-b8a2-1bdc14f86632-473188283-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-01-030121-ellen-tullos-1048444/',
                  null,
                  'tmz:video:2e5e28c6-cd9a-4fec-b8a2-1bdc14f86632',
                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }
      });
         </script>
        </section>

          wbq.push(function renderTwitterTweetBlock() {
  var response = 'unknown';
  var target = document.getElementById('cb-9e876716fc0716b51944a877b79f79ac-2145167694-target');

  function accept() {
    if (response === 'accepted') {
      return;
    }

    window.TMZ.utils.loadTwitterJs().then(function (twttr) {
      target.innerHTML = '';
      twttr.widgets.createTweet('1366454976441114629', target, {
        cards: '',
        conversation: '',
      });
    }).catch(reject);

    // there is no "accepted" html for twitter block, the above js does it all
    response = 'accepted';
  }

  function reject() {
    if (response === 'rejected') {
      return;
    }

    target.innerHTML = document.getElementById('cb-9e876716fc0716b51944a877b79f79ac-2145167694-rejected').innerHTML;
    response = 'rejected';
  }

  watchConsent(function (canUse) {
    canUse('twitter') ? accept() : reject();
  });
});
         </script>

          wbq.push(function renderYoutubeVideoBlock() {
      var $target = $('#cb-0e71451382d501ccccce80b7f855e47a-1906011529-target');
      var targetWidth = $target.width();

      function initPlayer(onReady) {
          new YT.Player('cb-0e71451382d501ccccce80b7f855e47a-1906011529-target', {
            height: targetWidth / (16 / 9),
            host: 'https://www.youtube-nocookie.com',
            width: targetWidth,
            events: {
              'onReady': onReady,
            },
            playerVars: {
              'enablejsapi': 1,
              'origin': window.location.origin,
            },
          });
      }

      function cueVideo(e) {
        e.target.cueVideoById('oYBFXPQ17Bc', 0);
      }

      function insertSwipe(e) {
        var swipeDiv = document.createElement('div');
        swipeDiv.innerText = "Exclusive";
        swipeDiv.classList.add('media-swipe');
        swipeDiv.classList.add('youtube-video-block__media-swipe');
        e.target.getIframe().parentNode.prepend(swipeDiv);
      }

      function fail() {
        $target.html(document.getElementById('cb-0e71451382d501ccccce80b7f855e47a-1906011529-failed').innerHTML);
      }

      function styleIframe(e) {
        var iframe = e.target.getIframe();
        iframe.classList.add('embed-responsive');
        if (!iframe.getAttribute('width')) {
          iframe.setAttribute('width', targetWidth);
        }
        if (!iframe.getAttribute('height')) {
          iframe.setAttribute('height', targetWidth / (16 / 9));
        }
      }

         <script>
          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-8515df8a-a233-4b72-b2b8-77531d71c879-149136278-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-8515df8a-a233-4b72-b2b8-77531d71c879-149136278-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-8515df8a-a233-4b72-b2b8-77531d71c879-149136278-footer');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-8515df8a-a233-4b72-b2b8-77531d71c879-149136278-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-8515df8a-a233-4b72-b2b8-77531d71c879-149136278-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-8515df8a-a233-4b72-b2b8-77531d71c879-149136278-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-8515df8a-a233-4b72-b2b8-77531d71c879-149136278-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-8515df8a-a233-4b72-b2b8-77531d71c879-149136278'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-8515df8a-a233-4b72-b2b8-77531d71c879-149136278-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-8515df8a-a233-4b72-b2b8-77531d71c879-149136278-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-02-030221-dr-oz-1048937/',
                  null,
                  'tmz:video:8515df8a-a233-4b72-b2b8-77531d71c879',
                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }
      });

          <strong class="updated-time--strong">
           11:24 AM PT
          </strong>
          -- Dr. Oz just detailed his lifesaving heroics at the airport ... and it's incredible.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-1176562038b1b8da5f9fd6aaa05b84c6-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default updated " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-e6f3b896000871a6f97b4f3a16001052">
         <p>
          Oz tells us the man who collapsed had no pulse, was turning a horrible color and had foam coming out of his mouth when he started doing CPR ... but things turned around when Oz was able to control the man's airway and the defibrillator arrived.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-e6f3b896000871a6f97b4f3a16001052-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default updated " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-3626d0cb83ec97914f493c38d5dd0ebf">
         <p>
          Dr. Oz says the defibrillator shocked the man at the highest power possible, and it worked ... in essence, bringing the man back from the dead!!!
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-3626d0cb83ec97914f493c38d5dd0ebf-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default updated " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-e592b50217f3eb4050f577f2940d1301">
         <p>
          Oz tells us why he couldn't have saved the man's life without the help of Port Authority police ... and our law enforcement sources confirmed the man was 60 years old and taken to a hospital, where there's been no update on his condition.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-e592b50217f3eb4050f577f2940d1301-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default updated " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-32cc98ffbccece8e5618d59e12bf86b8">
         <p>
          And, get this ... we're told Oz didn't tell the cop helping him exactly who he was, he just said he was a doctor.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-32cc98ffbccece8e5618d59e12bf86b8-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default updated " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-c8c89a98bba47d50631fe68af08673e6">
         <p>
          <strong class="updated-time--strong">
           10:39 AM PT
          </strong>
          -- We've obtained a photo from the scene of the medical emergency ... it's unclear if Oz is in the image, but you can see medical personnel around the man.
         </p>

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-6799c43025c8975135099b1de6a6e691">
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/dr-oz/">
           <strong>
            Dr. Oz
           </strong>
          </a>
          saved a life at the Newark airport after a man collapsed face down at baggage claim ... and the good doc was in the right place at the right time.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-6799c43025c8975135099b1de6a6e691-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-e1788794cbf9f6d34bd048f83456454e">
         <p>
          Sources close to Dr. Oz tells TMZ ... Oz rolled the man over Monday night, cleared his airway and began giving him CPR before using a defibrillator. We're told the guy flatlined and Oz shocked him back to life as a huge crowd watched.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-e1788794cbf9f6d34bd048f83456454e-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-74e48cbec823973077764025ce4f0fdf">
         <p>
          We're told there were no other doctors there, but a Port Authority police officer was there who helped Oz continue CPR while he cleared the man's airway.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-74e48cbec823973077764025ce4f0fdf-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-c78d6152ebcb72d99ea7319516a968a9">
         <p>
          It appears the man might have suffered a heart attack ... he's recovering at a New Jersey hospital and doing "okay" as he awaits test results. We're told Oz is in touch with the man's wife, who was traveling with him at the time.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-c78d6152ebcb72d99ea7319516a968a9-->

         <h2 class="article__header-title">
          <span class="article__hf1 text-uppercase h3">
           Snooki
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf2 text-uppercase h1">
           Never Say Never ...
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf3 text-none h2">
           Shooting 'Jersey Shore' Again!!!
          </span>
         </h2>
        </a>
        <h5 class="article__published-at">
         <ul class="social social--sm">
          <li class="social-item">

         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/74/4by3/2021/03/02/741d2f7672454d8a9d3de8223579d7d1_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="media-swipe image-block__media-swipe">
           Exclusive
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-21df3d56daa5f27638a243a24c659ae3-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-dd326e3082e115c26876919a0341413e">
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/snooki/">
           <strong>
            Snooki
           </strong>
          </a>
          's retirement from "Jersey Shore" was short-lived ... 'cause TMZ's learned she's filming again and we have some of the first images.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-dd326e3082e115c26876919a0341413e-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-729241cc9b4e05c24c7adbfcbbe9d061">
         <p>
          TMZ's obtained a picture that shows Snooki grabbing lunch with co-star
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/angelina-pivarnick/">
           <strong>
            Angelina
           </strong>
          </a>
          last week at Lucco Cucina + Bar in Florham Park, New Jersey. You can see a producer -- wearing a mask -- at a table next to them and we're told the restaurant was fully lit (for TV, not a party) as cameras rolled on their convo.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-729241cc9b4e05c24c7adbfcbbe9d061-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default " id="cb-66b6076b5ea5477ccbc894b3538cb1f7">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/70/4by3/2021/03/02/708778d870494f2cb543ce5018cfb170_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            TMZ.com
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-66b6076b5ea5477ccbc894b3538cb1f7-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-435ff19274fdd6774d5c50c7d5bb9bfa">
         <p>
          It's unclear how involved Snooki's gonna be in the MTV reality series -- guest appearance or full cast member -- but her shooting any scenes at all is significant because she
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2019/08/07/snooki-meltdown-screaming-leaves-jersey-shore-house-freaks-out/">
           <strong>
            swore off
           </strong>
          </a>
          all things 'Jersey Shore' back in December 2019. She told us as much back then when she even
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2019/12/12/snooki-jersey-shore-spin-off-family/">
           <strong>
            shot down
           </strong>
          </a>
          a possible spin-off.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-435ff19274fdd6774d5c50c7d5bb9bfa-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-84c3dfacadac7ad1915d4b5768a00c1e">
         <p>
          Also interesting is the pairing with Angelina -- true GTLers know they've almost always been at each other's throats since Day 1. That tension really amped up when Snooki,
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/deena-nicole-cortese/">
           <strong>
            Deena
           </strong>
          </a>
          and
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/jwoww/">
           <strong>
            JWOWW
           </strong>
          </a>
          took shots at Angelina during what was supposed to be a toast to her ... at her wedding!!!
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-84c3dfacadac7ad1915d4b5768a00c1e-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-youtube-video-block canvas-youtube-video-block-blogroll canvas-youtube-video-block--default " id="cb-1c074296966921c7f2a1c19a8c49494d">

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-1ff99afeb8c3c1f57e097ba802c56e44">
         <p>
          One theory ... Angelina recently made up with Jenni and Deena following the wedding fiasco. That backlash, btw, is part of the reason why Snooki quit the show -- so, it's possible the lunch was them squashing that beef.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-1ff99afeb8c3c1f57e097ba802c56e44-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-1888cf5503d9dbb59b215f470d4c020b">
         <p>
          Another theory ... it's an opportunity to promote her new TV gig as host of "Beach Cabana Royale" on Discovery+. Mama bear's gotta eat!!!
         </p>
        </section>

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default canvas-block-is-first " id="cb-3e4778f165755b796e85f957e498a8e9">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/b6/4by3/2021/03/02/b69249c6999e45068dd84229554ae511_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">

           </span>

        <!--/#cb-3e4778f165755b796e85f957e498a8e9-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-32a8e12a763d7491f4ddbf2d05fb5349">
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/bunny-wailer/">
           <strong>
            Bunny Wailer
           </strong>
          </a>
          -- the reggae icon and founding member of the original Wailers trio with
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/bob-marley/">
           <strong>
            Bob Marley
           </strong>
          </a>
          and
          <strong>
           Peter Tosh
          </strong>
          -- has died in Jamaica.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-32a8e12a763d7491f4ddbf2d05fb5349-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-a03aa2558af20f0f2cf1c0958b3f91fe">
         <p>
          Bunny, real name Neville Livingston, died Tuesday at the Medical Associates Hospital in Kingston ... according to his manager,
          <strong>
           Maxine Stowe
          </strong>
          . His cause of death's not been given, but he'd been dealing with serious medical issues since suffering his second stroke in 2020.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-a03aa2558af20f0f2cf1c0958b3f91fe-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default " id="cb-347d0127d0c0967794468972ebc1f8e1">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/e1/4by3/2021/03/02/e1d5b132511f4f999511ca578115481b_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            Getty
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-347d0127d0c0967794468972ebc1f8e1-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-af1e76f7dd1e3dbd7d9e22c6717808d8">
         <p>
          Born in Jamaica, Livingston befriended Marley at a young age and they'd go on to form the legendary reggae group with Tosh. Though Marley and Tosh were the primary singers and songwriters ... Bunny was known for his incredible harmonies on their songs.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-af1e76f7dd1e3dbd7d9e22c6717808d8-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-0a691081417f270a83c66b2f1c632050">
         <p>
          In 1965 the trio released their debut album, "The Wailing Wailers," before going on hiatus and reuniting again in the '70s. Around that time, Bunny wrote and recorded one of his most famous songs, "Dreamland" ... which he later released on his solo album, "Blackheart Man," in 1976.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-0a691081417f270a83c66b2f1c632050-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-youtube-video-block canvas-youtube-video-block-blogroll canvas-youtube-video-block--default " id="cb-40fac194810c6f63ea4d2b9e64f277b0">
         <div class="d-flex justify-content-center" id="cb-40fac194810c6f63ea4d2b9e64f277b0-1306468027-target">
         </div>
         <script id="cb-40fac194810c6f63ea4d2b9e64f277b0-1306468027-failed" type="text/x-consent-element">
          <p><strong>Unable to render YouTube Video.</strong></p>
         </script>

        <!--/#cb-40fac194810c6f63ea4d2b9e64f277b0-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-4a61b4bef950b86bee0de590a5a3756d">
         <p>
          The Wailers achieved international fame in 1973 with the release of "Catch a Fire" and follow-up album "Burnin'" ... but this would ultimately lead to the group splitting up.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-4a61b4bef950b86bee0de590a5a3756d-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-87353b210ecafd95515a78836cfc39b0">
         <p>
          Bunny and Tosh both left the band in 1974, but Bunny would be forever linked to the rise of reggae along with Marley ... and had a successful solo career himself. He'd go on to work with Jamaican musicians,
          <strong>
           Sly
          </strong>
          and
          <strong>
           Robbie
          </strong>
          , and produce albums of several other artists.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-87353b210ecafd95515a78836cfc39b0-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-22c2f5005583d44ec7437cc16e3ec778">
         <p>
          Bunny won a Grammy for Best Reggae Album in 1991 for "Time Will Tell: A Tribute to Bob Marley," and would go on to win 2 more ... including another tribute album in 1997.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-22c2f5005583d44ec7437cc16e3ec778-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-427c6e54d061e6c8a330f7fb8ea1d24f">
         <p>
          As for other awards ... he received the Order of Merit from the Jamaican government in 2017 for his contributions and achievements. Bunny last toured in 2016 for the 40th anniversary of "Blackheart Man."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-427c6e54d061e6c8a330f7fb8ea1d24f-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-feaea41f229a463d395ccb551cfe5987">
         <p>
          He was the last remaining member of the OG Wailers. Marley died of cancer in 1981, and Tosh was murdered by gunmen in an attempted robbery at his home in 1987.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-feaea41f229a463d395ccb551cfe5987-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-2f58f22d1fd5f9c37a75d7993f0ad29c">
         <p>
          Bunny was 73.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-2f58f22d1fd5f9c37a75d7993f0ad29c-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-5952bcce218791c4e1a1c3dc2322aaa4">
         <p>
          RIP
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-5952bcce218791c4e1a1c3dc2322aaa4-->

         <h2 class="article__header-title">
          <span class="article__hf1 text-uppercase h3">
           Kodak Black
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf2 text-uppercase h1">
           Judge Gives Him the Okay to Travel
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf3 text-none h2">
           ... But Only for Work
          </span>
         </h2>
        </a>

         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/64/4by3/2021/03/02/64475e99df8f46f584589e7e1d47a93e_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="media-swipe image-block__media-swipe">
           Exclusive
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-8114dbf3b5433b4937325fdc166a9e47-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-358da99bb0265eef9d7ff689ba2d135e">
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/kodak-black/">
           <strong>
            Kodak Black
           </strong>
          </a>
          is on the move -- or he's about to be anyway, because a judge just signed off on him being able to pack up and hit the road ... with limitations, of course.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-358da99bb0265eef9d7ff689ba2d135e-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-eadbdfcd0a334073c488e34a12dbc03d">
         <p>
          A federal judge just approved Kodak's motion to travel for work purposes only -- giving him the green light to go out of state ... so long as he lets 'em know exactly where he's going.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-eadbdfcd0a334073c488e34a12dbc03d-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-d6b4e2c4e9ad3e9bcbea097294cf69fc">
         <p>
          According to the legal docs, obtained by TMZ, the judge says KB has to provide a full itinerary to his probation officer, including where he'll be staying during the travel. Naturally, he'll also have to keep his nose clean while out and about.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-d6b4e2c4e9ad3e9bcbea097294cf69fc-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-video-block canvas-video-block-blogroll canvas-video-block--default " id="cb-e16e9dbe6751940c96ac481ece00d620">

          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-f7ed26cd-61d7-4d75-b70e-e824e1573d8a-1046901075-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-f7ed26cd-61d7-4d75-b70e-e824e1573d8a-1046901075-footer');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-f7ed26cd-61d7-4d75-b70e-e824e1573d8a-1046901075-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-f7ed26cd-61d7-4d75-b70e-e824e1573d8a-1046901075-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-f7ed26cd-61d7-4d75-b70e-e824e1573d8a-1046901075-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-f7ed26cd-61d7-4d75-b70e-e824e1573d8a-1046901075-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-f7ed26cd-61d7-4d75-b70e-e824e1573d8a-1046901075'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-f7ed26cd-61d7-4d75-b70e-e824e1573d8a-1046901075-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-f7ed26cd-61d7-4d75-b70e-e824e1573d8a-1046901075-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-02-15-021521-kodak-black-1041248/',
                  null,
                  'tmz:video:f7ed26cd-61d7-4d75-b70e-e824e1573d8a',
                  null,
                  {
                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });
              hideSpinner();
            }
                      });
        }
      });
         </script>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-e16e9dbe6751940c96ac481ece00d620-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-9f879387e9911479c038fd1de1961aa3">
         <p>
          In his original filing seeking the OK for this, Kodak's attorneys said his plans were to continue the charitable work he's been engaged in lately -- specifically citing the scholarship he set up in the name of one of the Parkland victims,
          <strong>
           Meadow Pollack
          </strong>
          , which he recently
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/02/15/kodak-black-msdhs-parkland-victims-meadow-pollack-scholarsihp/">
           <strong>
            commemorated with a public service
           </strong>
          </a>
          .
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-9f879387e9911479c038fd1de1961aa3-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-5b53470c7687d4c990ff0e9427e8516d">
         <p>
          It's interesting ... Kodak's attorney,
          <strong>
           Bradford Cohen
          </strong>
          , tells TMZ that in addition to the philanthropy, Kodak will also be attending to his music biz as well. We're told he might be looking to book some concert appearances -- when that's possible again -- and record label meetings.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-5b53470c7687d4c990ff0e9427e8516d-->
       </div>
