      <article class="article" id="blogroll-e7352905-bae9-457f-845a-5a297793f514">
       <div class="article__channel--reporting">
       </div>
       <header class="article__header">
        <a class="article__header-link js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"headline","pos":12}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:e7352905-bae9-457f-845a-5a297793f514" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/02/dr-seuss-books-racist-imagery-biden-print/">
         <h2 class="article__header-title">
          <span class="article__hf1 text-uppercase h3">
           Dr. Seuss
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf2 text-uppercase h1">
           6 Books No Longer Published ...
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf3 text-none h2">
           Due to Racist Imagery
          </span>
         </h2>
        </a>
        <h5 class="article__published-at">
         <ul class="social social--sm">
          <li class="social-item">
           <a aria-label="Share on Facebook" class="btn social__btn social__btn--sm social__btn--facebook js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"facebook-header","pos":12}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:e7352905-bae9-457f-845a-5a297793f514" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/02/dr-seuss-books-racist-imagery-biden-print/" onclick="window.open('http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tmz.com%2F2021%2F03%2F02%2Fdr-seuss-books-racist-imagery-biden-print%2F', '_blank', 'status=0,width=575,height=450');return false;">
            <span aria-label="Facebook" class="icon icon-facebook--white social__icon--facebook" role="img">
            </span>
            <span class="social__count">
             12.4K
            </span>
            <span class="sr-only">
             shares
            </span>
           </a>
          </li>
          <li class="social-item">
           <a aria-label="Share on Twitter" class="btn social__btn social__btn--sm social__btn--twitter js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"twitter-header","pos":12}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:e7352905-bae9-457f-845a-5a297793f514" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/02/dr-seuss-books-racist-imagery-biden-print/" onclick="window.open('https://twitter.com/intent/tweet?url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tmz.com%2F2021%2F03%2F02%2Fdr-seuss-books-racist-imagery-biden-print%2F&amp;text=6%20Dr.%20Seuss%20Books%20Won%27t%20Be%20Published%20Anymore%20Due%20to%20Racist%20Imagery&amp;via=TMZ&amp;related=HarveyLevinTMZ', '_blank', 'status=0,width=575,height=450');return false;">
            <span aria-label="Twitter" class="icon icon-sd icon-twitter--white" role="img">
            </span>
           </a>
          </li>
         </ul>
         <!--/.social-->
         3/2/2021 6:35 AM PT
        </h5>
        <!--/.article__posted-date-->
       </header>
       <div class="article__blocks">
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default canvas-block-is-first " id="cb-1ae35c2f267ca89d2a272867f0adf58f">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/4a/4by3/2021/03/02/4aca5c4b1aec4045b1983c727c8d7891_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            Getty
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-1ae35c2f267ca89d2a272867f0adf58f-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-40f53e8eeaa6cdf35abbdab07eba0ae6">
         <p>
          <strong>
           Dr. Seuss
          </strong>
          books have been beloved by children and adults for generations, but 6 of them will no longer be published because they are racially offensive ... according to the business that preserves the author's legacy.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-40f53e8eeaa6cdf35abbdab07eba0ae6-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-acfebdb8562cc15e6c97229fefb4c2eb">
         <p>
          Dr. Seuss Enterprises says these 6 Seuss books -- including "And to Think That I Saw It on Mulberry Street" and "Scrambled Eggs Super!" -- "portray people in ways that are hurtful and wrong."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-acfebdb8562cc15e6c97229fefb4c2eb-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default " id="cb-a48041a1e6653fdcd0b657b60f7a3ad3">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/4c/4by3/2021/03/02/4ccfda476d414498baa71bc461a4b6de_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            Vanguard Press/Random House
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-a48041a1e6653fdcd0b657b60f7a3ad3-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-3065d019a94fad36961ad43cdff942de">
         <p>
          The company says it made the decision to cease sales on these books -- which also include "If I Ran the Zoo," "McElligots Pool," "On Beyond Zebra!" and "The Cats Quizzer" -- after consulting with educators and reviewing its catalog.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-3065d019a94fad36961ad43cdff942de-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default " id="cb-ef394a8a6d0d04ef040a2f2dbaf2de17">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/d9/4by3/2021/03/02/d9c0f0c82da147abb2ff819f28f6bd2d_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            Vanguard Press/Random House
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-ef394a8a6d0d04ef040a2f2dbaf2de17-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-c2d523111e9422e2198db1a2c0fec3d1">
         <p>
          The announcement was made on Tuesday, March 2 -- Dr. Seuss's birthday -- though the decision was made last year. The move comes as President
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/joe-biden/">
           <strong>
            Biden
           </strong>
          </a>
          also omitted mention of Dr. Seuss on Read Across America Day ... which is held annually on the author's bday.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-c2d523111e9422e2198db1a2c0fec3d1-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-28966fefa38edd637cf289d1f53feeba">
         <p>
          Dr. Seuss -- born Theodor Seuss Geisel -- has come under increased scrutiny over the years as his history of racist and anti-Semitic work has been uncovered. A study of 50 Seuss books in 2019 found 43 of 45 characters of color had characteristics aligning with "Orientalism" and 2 "African" characters had anti-Black qualities.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-28966fefa38edd637cf289d1f53feeba-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-ca386db471b81a52961d1ed5c2a8f937">
         <p>
          Of the 6 books being pulled ... "The Cat's Quizzer" and "If I Ran the Zoo" were cited in the study specifically for examples of Orientalism and white supremacy.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-ca386db471b81a52961d1ed5c2a8f937-->
       </div>
       <!--/.article__blocks-->

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default updated " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-36a8d909b5488051465347b9acffa1d7">
         <p>
          <strong class="updated-time--strong">
           8:59 AM PT
          </strong>
          --
          <strong>
           TMZ Sports
          </strong>
          has obtained photos of all three cars involved in the crash ... and the images are horrifying.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-36a8d909b5488051465347b9acffa1d7-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default updated " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-015edc5f5cb5a11e7543e0c2f57a88ab">
         <p>
          The pictures show major damage to all 3 cars -- and it's a miracle no one was killed.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-015edc5f5cb5a11e7543e0c2f57a88ab-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default updated " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-da3873f8d3cc01f9a01438f8872a5929">
         <p>
          In the photos, you can see the front of Reid's white pickup truck was completely smashed in. The car Young was in, meanwhile, had its third-row caved in by the violent contact.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-da3873f8d3cc01f9a01438f8872a5929-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default updated " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-b68b31b12c8c94939737334c3534e110">
         <p>
          The photos show the third car also suffered significant damage to its front end.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-b68b31b12c8c94939737334c3534e110-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-a278839eddcd67b2c955c8d13cdb1368">
         <p>
          The little girl injured in the
          <strong>
           Britt Reid
          </strong>
          car wreck likely has permanent brain damage and will be confined to a wheelchair for the foreseeable future, her family lawyer says.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-a278839eddcd67b2c955c8d13cdb1368-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-223bb7431e8c8e4e7c66b4892944966d">
         <p>
          The attorney for the family of 5-year-old
          <strong>
           Ariel Young
          </strong>
          appeared on "Good Morning America" with an update on her health ... and it's not great.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-223bb7431e8c8e4e7c66b4892944966d-->

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-50587c8017c722fa91bd214ba6c67d45">
         <p>
          Attorney
          <strong>
           Tom Porto
          </strong>
          explained she's
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/02/16/ariel-young-wakes-from-coma-britt-reid-crash-kc-chiefs/">
           <strong>
            awake from her coma
           </strong>
          </a>
          but has suffered very serious injuries that will affect her for the rest of her life.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-50587c8017c722fa91bd214ba6c67d45-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-840fa192ebb013d0329d79cf77e5ed73">
         <p>
          "Shes awake, which is a huge development, Porto said ... "She likely has permanent brain damage that she will endure for the rest of her life. Shes not walking -- its a sad, sad, sad story."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-840fa192ebb013d0329d79cf77e5ed73-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-c9bba4c259057eca0b33a60c209a8a47">
         <p>
          Porto also released images of the crash scene to ABC News showing Reid's white truck completely smashed in on the front side of the ride. It appears the truck was moving at a high speed when the collision occurred.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-c9bba4c259057eca0b33a60c209a8a47-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-ad8926b375bd40ade1ef92324e768270">
         <p>
          Reid -- an assistant coach for the KC Chiefs at the time -- allegedly
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/02/05/britt-reid-andy-reid-car-crash-kansas-city-chiefs-super-bowl/">
           <strong>
            slammed his truck
           </strong>
          </a>
          into two cars that were parked on the side of the road on Feb. 4, badly injuring Ariel Young.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-ad8926b375bd40ade1ef92324e768270-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-4b047258bfe6842bd670da7ca2f73df7">
         <p>
          Young's family had driven to the scene to help another family member who was stranded on the side of the road after running out of gas.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-4b047258bfe6842bd670da7ca2f73df7-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-51018ab74194c3fc41b8b4619c9abbf0">
         <p>
          All three of the cars involved in the wreck suffered severe damage -- and it's a miracle no one was killed.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-51018ab74194c3fc41b8b4619c9abbf0-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-3a7d1faa0cfeb04407723a4f5631bb52">
         <p>
          As for Ariel Young, Porto says she had a long road ahead of her when it comes to her recovery.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-3a7d1faa0cfeb04407723a4f5631bb52-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-021341a013ea0a48418163ff8e70a9c9">
         <p>
          Porto told ABC News the family wants Reid -- son of KC Chiefs head coach
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/andy-reid/">
           <strong>
            Andy Reid
           </strong>
          </a>
          -- prosecuted to the full extent of the law.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-021341a013ea0a48418163ff8e70a9c9-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default " id="cb-3342b7a3d60f633a907ff5beba5cff49">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/88/4by3/2021/03/02/884c58c4b6ef4fc990461b9cf631b5be_md.jpg"/>
          <div class="image-block__card-footer">
           <span class="media-credit image-block__media-credit">
            Getty
           </span>
          </div>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-3342b7a3d60f633a907ff5beba5cff49-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-6a26412ef2a5af1f9e16350de2e3d2ff">
         <p>
          Porto cites a police report in which Reid allegedly admitted to consuming 2 to 3 alcoholic beverages -- and taking the prescription medication Adderall -- before getting behind the wheel that fateful day.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-6a26412ef2a5af1f9e16350de2e3d2ff-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-27c42a28916e6ec31262bb78c2f808d1">
         <p>
          Porto said the family is hoping prosecutors hit Reid with felony DWI charges.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-27c42a28916e6ec31262bb78c2f808d1-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default canvas-block-is-last " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-2c2de9c6c90eda622fc09f4de07f2ab4">

        <a class="article__header-link js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"headline","pos":14}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:33c2f2eb-4a42-4578-a310-7789351552f1" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/02/britney-spears-and-teenage-sons-photos-posts/">
         <h2 class="article__header-title">
          <span class="article__hf1 text-uppercase h3">
           Britney Spears
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf2 text-uppercase h1">
           Posts Rare Pic with Her Boys ...
          </span>
          <span class="article__hf3 text-none h2">
           'I'm Extremely Lucky'
          </span>
         </h2>
        </a>
        <h5 class="article__published-at">
         <ul class="social social--sm">
          <li class="social-item">
           <a aria-label="Share on Facebook" class="btn social__btn social__btn--sm social__btn--facebook js-track-link" data-context='{"section":"main","name":"facebook-header","pos":14}' data-node-ref="tmz:article:33c2f2eb-4a42-4578-a310-7789351552f1" data-widget-ref="tmz:blogroll-widget:39cc321d-66b9-57e0-816e-f745a6fcb489" href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/03/02/britney-spears-and-teenage-sons-photos-posts/" onclick="window.open('http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.tmz.com%2F2021%2F03%2F02%2Fbritney-spears-and-teenage-sons-photos-posts%2F', '_blank', 'status=0,width=575,height=450');return false;">

       <div class="article__blocks">
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default canvas-block-is-first " id="cb-75b6d84f0241aa3e3a561a20f48438f4">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/31/4by3/2021/03/02/31d6d0d2593a44d2a69cc3255e082159_md.jpg"/>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-75b6d84f0241aa3e3a561a20f48438f4-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-30bfaa947dfc21e0a783b7d28a190d22">
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/britney-spears/">
           <strong>
            Britney Spears
           </strong>
          </a>
          got some quality time in with her teenage sons ... and shared a rare photo of them all together as a memento.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-30bfaa947dfc21e0a783b7d28a190d22-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-1932049821444ea8324047f3f49fcb16">
         <p>
          Britney posted the pic Monday of her and her 2 boys -- 15-year-old
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/sean-preston/">
           <strong>
            Sean
           </strong>
          </a>
          and 14-year-old
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/jayden-james/">
           <strong>
            Jayden
           </strong>
          </a>
          -- standing in an open field together ... and she looks happy as can be.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-1932049821444ea8324047f3f49fcb16-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-fff465b30bc72f8d0d9f95c5b0221415">
         <p>
          She marveled at how big her kids are now and how time flies, saying ... "it's very hard for any mama especially a mama with boys seeing them grow up so fast !!!!"
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-fff465b30bc72f8d0d9f95c5b0221415-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-image-block canvas-image-block-blogroll canvas-image-block--default " id="cb-f108c1979e2dc881d471d8259a8ff540">
         <div class="image-block">
          <img alt="" class="img-fluid image-block__img-fluid img-aspect-auto" loading="lazy" src="https://imagez.tmz.com/image/5b/4by3/2021/03/02/5b9981502a7940998df1f17e9a371a7f_md.jpg"/>
         </div>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-f108c1979e2dc881d471d8259a8ff540-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-14885121daa7e33712afb567b72feb12">
         <p>
          Brit's also very proud of her sons, adding ... "I'm extremely lucky because my two babies are such gentleman and so kind that I must have done something right !!!!"
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-14885121daa7e33712afb567b72feb12-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-d1d3f44b2e36aa512317a9965478a41b">
         <p>
          The singer says she hasn't posted any photos of Sean or Jayden in a while because -- well, they're teenagers -- but they let her post this one ... including an edited version with a more intense background.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-d1d3f44b2e36aa512317a9965478a41b-->

         <p>

          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/kevin-federline/">
           <strong>
            Kevin Federline
           </strong>

           <strong>

          .

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-7fd3838f8b63ca9a2ce7b0d6b0dbb9e2">
         <p>
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/zlatan-ibrahimovic/">
           <strong>
            Zlatan Ibrahimovic
           </strong>
          </a>
          is not backing down from his criticism of
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/people/lebron-james/">
           <strong>
            LeBron James
           </strong>
          </a>
          -- reinforcing his belief that athletes should stick to sports and stay out of politics!
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-7fd3838f8b63ca9a2ce7b0d6b0dbb9e2-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-706069b891df26e1e6c046d1ae05008b">
         <p>
          "Athletes unite the world, politics divide it, the soccer superstar said at a news conference Tuesday morning.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-706069b891df26e1e6c046d1ae05008b-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-7895063cd808f6ed94e699f977206254">
         <p>
          "Our role is to unite the world by doing what we do best. Athletes should be athletes and politicians should do politics."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-7895063cd808f6ed94e699f977206254-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-youtube-video-block canvas-youtube-video-block-blogroll canvas-youtube-video-block--default " id="cb-9b983fccbda857b9a03051a124b6e29a">

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-3544354154976f08e3bab0ca92470d6c">
         <p>
          Ibra -- one of the most famous athletes on the planet -- has been under fire for
          <a href="https://www.tmz.com/2021/02/25/zlatan-ibrahimovic-lebron-james-stay-out-of-politics-do-what-youre-good-at/">
           <strong>
            going after LeBron
           </strong>
          </a>
          last week during an interview with Discovery+ in Sweden.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-3544354154976f08e3bab0ca92470d6c-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-8a5d63e507b397d7448b7f5bc933c960">
         <p>
          At the time, Zlatan said, "[LeBron] is phenomenal at what he's doing, but I don't like when people have some kind of status, they go and do politics at the same time."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-8a5d63e507b397d7448b7f5bc933c960-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-590e3b43a165b805a6663fe5d2eab469">
         <p>
          "Do what you're good at. Do the category you do. I play football because I'm the best at playing football."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-590e3b43a165b805a6663fe5d2eab469-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-e02d60870e5aa79eeaa5b00ab09628da">
         <p>
          "I don't do politics. If I would be a political politician, I would do politics. That is the first mistake people do when they become famous and they become in a certain status. Stay out of it. Just do what you do best, because it doesn't look good."
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-e02d60870e5aa79eeaa5b00ab09628da-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-ca650fbb25cf8633882d84ae8121b75c">
         <p>
          LeBron clapped back in a big way -- saying he'll NEVER just shut up and dribble because he understands his voice can make a real impact for those who aren't being heard ... and feels it's his responsibility to use his platform to make positive change.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-ca650fbb25cf8633882d84ae8121b75c-->

         <script>
          wbq.push(function renderVideoBlock() {
        var page = window.TMZ.select(window.TMZ.selectors.getPage);
        // there is a weird bug with iPhone 6+ on iOS 9.3.4 where the spinner gets revealed even after its
        // event listener has been removed, so for now this stupid flag can correct for that.
        var isResolved = false;
        if (!page.isTurbolinksPreview) {
          function displayPlayer(player) {
            if (player.id === 'jwplayer-video-player-06b2c493-daf4-439b-af8b-cb8b3716a76d-1278824840-player') {
              player.getContainer().closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
              return;
            }
            // a fallback video
            player.closest('.embed-responsive-item--jwplayer').classList.remove('invisible');
          }
          function fadeImageHolderAndFooter() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-06b2c493-daf4-439b-af8b-cb8b3716a76d-1278824840-image-holder');
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-06b2c493-daf4-439b-af8b-cb8b3716a76d-1278824840-footer');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.addEventListener('transitionend', removeImageHolder, { once: true });
              imageHolder.classList.add('video-block__image-holder-fade');
            }

            if (footer && !footer.classList.contains('hidden')) {
              footer.addEventListener('transitionend', removeFooter, { once: true });
              footer.classList.add('video-block__media-footer-fade');
            }
          }
          function removeImageHolder() {
            var imageHolder = document.getElementById('video-player-06b2c493-daf4-439b-af8b-cb8b3716a76d-1278824840-image-holder');
            if (imageHolder) {
              imageHolder.remove();
            }
          }
          function removeFooter() {
            var footer = document.getElementById('video-player-06b2c493-daf4-439b-af8b-cb8b3716a76d-1278824840-footer');
            if (footer) {
              footer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
          }
          function hideSpinner() {
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-06b2c493-daf4-439b-af8b-cb8b3716a76d-1278824840-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('below');
            spinner.classList.remove('above');
          }
          function revealSpinner() {
            if (isResolved) {
              return;
            }
            var spinner = document.getElementById('video-player-06b2c493-daf4-439b-af8b-cb8b3716a76d-1278824840-progress-spinner');
            spinner.classList.add('above');
            spinner.classList.remove('below');
          }
          window.TMZ.videos.observe(document.getElementById('jwplayer-video-player-06b2c493-daf4-439b-af8b-cb8b3716a76d-1278824840'), {
                        onObserve: function() {
              document.getElementById('video-player-06b2c493-daf4-439b-af8b-cb8b3716a76d-1278824840-play-btn').addEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner, { once: true });
            },
            onResolve: function(player) {
              isResolved = true;
              var playButton = document.getElementById('video-player-06b2c493-daf4-439b-af8b-cb8b3716a76d-1278824840-play-btn');
              playButton.removeEventListener('mousemove', revealSpinner);
              playButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
                displayPlayer(player);
                player.play();
                removeImageHolder();
                removeFooter();
                window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.clickLink(
                  'https://www.tmz.com/videos/2021-03-01-030121-laney-keyz-v3-1048556/',

                    section: 'blogroll',
                    name: 'video',
                    action: 'click'
                  }
                ));
              }, { once: true });

            }
                      });

        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-132a6c0680fc14635a5e6ed074063db4">
         <p>
          Bay Area rapper
          <strong>
           Laney Keyz
          </strong>
          's home got riddled with bullets and it wasn't a drive-by ... it was a walk-up, and it was all captured on some wild video.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-132a6c0680fc14635a5e6ed074063db4-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-11e233e1c7f8403feb98e81e5ae279e9">
         <p>
          TMZ has obtained surveillance footage that shows three men walk up to what we're told was Laney's L.A. home in the wee hours of Feb. 18 ... and you see them fire off several rounds at the property before they turn around and make a run for it.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-11e233e1c7f8403feb98e81e5ae279e9-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-2e07a0c0b39f7569858a0fa7005231b2">
         <p>
          One of the guys seems to linger to shoot a bit more ... and eventually scrams with his cohorts. It doesn't appear anyone returned fire -- even though they react like that happened.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-2e07a0c0b39f7569858a0fa7005231b2-->
        <section class="canvas-block canvas-block-blogroll canvas-text-block canvas-text-block-blogroll canvas-text-block--default " data-context='{"section":"blogroll","name":"text_block"}' id="cb-8ab4703d072085596e1d81c2f61617de">
         <p>
          Anyway, law enforcement sources tell us LAPD officers located a number of shell casings on the ground where the shooting was reported, but theyve come up empty thus far on possible suspects. Fortunately, we're told no one was injured in the gunfire ... an investigation's underway.
         </p>
        </section>
        <!--/#cb-8ab4703d072085596e1d81c2f61617de-->

          wbq.push(function renderYoutubeVideoBlock() {
      var $target = $('#cb-3602da06e306f66c50f469006ca00d70-1488314421-target');
      var targetWidth = $target.width();

      function initPlayer(onReady) {
          new YT.Player('cb-3602da06e306f66c50f469006ca00d70-1488314421-target', {
            height: targetWidth / (16 / 9),
            host: 'https://www.youtube-nocookie.com',
            width: targetWidth,
            events: {
              'onReady': onReady,
            },
            playerVars: {
              'enablejsapi': 1,
              'origin': window.location.origin,
            },
          });
      }

      function cueVideo(e) {
        e.target.cueVideoById('VKF3y6_Dlnw', 0);
      }

      function insertSwipe(e) {
        var swipeDiv = document.createElement('div');
        swipeDiv.innerText = "Exclusive";
        swipeDiv.classList.add('media-swipe');
        swipeDiv.classList.add('youtube-video-block__media-swipe');
        e.target.getIframe().parentNode.prepend(swipeDiv);
      }

      function fail() {
        $target.html(document.getElementById('cb-3602da06e306f66c50f469006ca00d70-1488314421-failed').innerHTML);
      }

      function styleIframe(e) {
        var iframe = e.target.getIframe();
        iframe.classList.add('embed-responsive');
        if (!iframe.getAttribute('width')) {
          iframe.setAttribute('width', targetWidth);
        }
        if (!iframe.getAttribute('height')) {
          iframe.setAttribute('height', targetWidth / (16 / 9));
        }
      }

              window.TMZ.utils.loadYouTubeJs()
          .then(function initYouTubeBlock() {
            initPlayer(function onReady(e) {
              styleIframe(e);
              cueVideo(e);
                                        });
          }).catch(fail);
          });

Parton","image_ref":"tmz:image-asset:image_jpg_20141023_9105edbd01a856789f40de0b6d33f828","bio":"<p>Dolly Rebecca Parton (born January 19, 1946) is an American singer-songwriter, author, multi-instrumentalist, actress and philanthropist, best-known for her work in country music. In the four-and-a-half decades since her national-chart d\u00e9but, she remains one of the most-successful female artists in the history of the country genre which garnered her the title of 'The Queen of Country Music', with twenty-five number-one singles, and a record forty-one top-10 country albums. She has the distinction of having performed on a top-five country hit in each of the last five decades and is tied with Reba McEntire as the only country artists with No. 1 singles in four consecutive decades. She is known for her distinctive soprano, sometimes bawdy humor, flamboyant dress sense and voluptuous figure. Childhood Dolly Parton was born in Sevierville, Tennessee, the fourth of twelve children born: Her family was, as she described them, \"dirt poor\". She described her family's shortness of money in a number of her early songs, notably \"Coat of Many Colors\" which happens to be her favorite, still today, to sing over all of her others, and \"In the Good Old Days (When Times Were Bad)\". They lived in a rustic, dilapidated one-room cabin in Locust Ridge, Tennessee, a hamlet just north of the Greenbrier Valley in the Great Smoky Mountains of Sevier County, a predominantly Pentecostal area. Music formed a major part of her early church experience. Spears. She was raised in Kentwood, LA. Spears has an older brother, Bryan, and a younger sister, Jamie Lynn. She\u2019s been married twice. Her first husband was childhood friend Jason Alexander in 2004 in Las Vegas. Their union was annulled after only 55 hours. Spears was then married to backup dancer Kevin Federline from 2004-2006. They have two sons together, Sean Preston (born September 14, 2005) and Jayden James (born September 12, 2006). She also dotes on her nieces, Jamie Lynn\u2019s daughter, Maddie, and Bryan\u2019s daughter, Sophia. Aside from her marriages, Spears has been involved in several relationships that didn\u2019t make it to the altar. Her most high profile romance was undoubtedly with childhood sweetheart and \u201cMickey Mouse Club\u201d co-star Justin Timberlake. They affectionately called one another \u201cPinky\u201d and \u201cStinky.\u201d She split from fiance, agent Jason Trawick, in January 2013. Spears has also dated producer Charlie Ebersol, David Lucado, paparazzo Adnan Ghalib, and Sam Asghari.<\/p>\n<p>Spears was destined for stardom as a child. She appeared on \u201cStar Search\u201d in 1992 at age 11. Disney\u2019s \u201cThe All New Mickey Mouse Club\u201d was a breedinground for some of today\u2019s biggest stars in the early \u201890s. The show not only introduced us to Spears, but also to her co-stars Justin Timberlake, J.C. Chasez, Christina Aguilera, Ryan Gosling, and Keri Russell. Spears shot to fame with the hit single and album \u201c\u2026Baby One More Time\u201d in 1998 after the teenager signed with Jive Records. Her follow-up albums include \u201cOops!... I Did It Again,\u201d \u201cBritney,\u201d \u201cIn the Zone,\u201d \u201cBlackout,\u201d \u201cCircus,\u201d \u201cFemme Fatale,\u201d \u201cBritney Jean,\u201d and \u201cGlory.\u201d Some of her best known songs are \u201cCrazy,\u201d \u201cToxic,\u201d and \u201cWomanizer.\u201d She toured the world to promote her music. After four years at The AXIS at Planet Hollywood Resort and Casino, Spears\u2019 Las Vegas concert residency \u201cPiece of Me\u201d is coming to a close on New Year\u2019s Eve 2017. She was presented with the Michael Jackson Video Vanguard Award at the 2011 MTV Video Music Awards, received the Millennium Award at the 2016 Billboard Music Awards, and was honored with the Icon Award at the 2017 Radio Disney Music Awards. She won a Grammy for best dance recording for her hit track \u201cToxic\u201d in 2004. Spears served on \u201cThe X Factor\u201d judging panel for one season in 2012. She also showed us her acting chops with guest spots on the television shows \u201cHow I Met Your Mother\u201d and \u201cGlee\u201d and in the lead role in the movie \u201cCrossroads.\u201d Spears has been known to pop in to teach kids\u2019 dance classes from time to time in the Los Angeles area. She\u2019s also put her name on such products as fragrances and lingerie.<\/p>\n<p>Spears\u2019 career and life are hotter than ever, but flashback to a few years ago and things were not as bright. She suffered a mental breakdown of epic proportions. In 2006, her parenting skills were called into question after driving with her son on her lap. Then, she began partying hard and was caught going commando after filing for divorce. In 2007, things went from bad to worse. Spears checked in and out of rehab numerous times, shaved her head, and attacked a paparazzo with an umbrella. At the MTV VMAs in September, Spears appeared lost, intoxicated, and unrehearsed during her performance of \u201cGimme More.\u201d Then, at the beginning of January 2008, she was taken out of her home on a stretcher after locking herself in the bathroom with one of her sons. Wallet ever since a conservatorship was put in place in After playing for a local Swedish Club for a couple of years he transferred to Malm\u00f6 FF in his teens, and it was here he started to pursue a career as a professional footballer.\n\nZlatan progressed through Malm\u00f6 FF's youth academy and his breakthrough at senior level came during the 1999-2000 season when he played for Malm\u00f6 FF's first team under coach Roland Andersson. Zlatan surprised Sweden with his superb technique and great goal scoring ability. As a determined 18 year-old he had already at this point decided that he was going to play for Sweden in the World Cup 2002 in Japan and Korea.\n\nAfter being perused by top Clubs all over the world, Zlatan finally decided to transfer to Ajax and he joined the Amsterdam club in July 2001. He received the number 9 shirt, which was previously worn by Nwankwo Kanu, Patrick Kluivert and the legendary Marco van Basten. After playing for Sweden's Under-21s, the Swedish National Team managers Tommy S\u00f6derberg and Lars Lagerb\u00e4ck chose Zlatan to play his International debut against the Faroe Islands in Sweden in January 2001, and since then Zlatan has been a part of the Swedish National Team.\n\nZlatan ended his first season at Ajax, just like he started it, on top. He scored the golden goal in the Dutch Cup Final against Utrecht and Ajax won both the League and the Cup.    <script>
    wbq.push(function manageSearchScreen() {
  var $search = $('.js__search-screen');
  var $searchCloseBtn = $('#search-screen-close-btn');
  var $searchToggleBtn = $('.js__btn--search-toggle');
  var $mastheadSearchOpenBtn = $('#masthead-search-open-btn');
  var $nav = $('.js__nav');

  function lockSearchFocus() {
    $searchCloseBtn.focus();
    document.addEventListener('focusin', focusSearchCloseBtn);
  }

  function focusSearchCloseBtn(event) {
    if (!$.contains(document.getElementById('search-screen'), event.target)) {
      $searchCloseBtn.focus();
    }
  }

  function unlockSearchFocus() {
    document.removeEventListener('focusin', focusSearchCloseBtn);
    $mastheadSearchOpenBtn.focus();
  }

  // close X used to dismiss mobile search overlay
  $searchToggleBtn.click(function (event) {
    // Toggle search screen visibility
    $search.toggleClass('search-screen--is-open');

    if ($search.hasClass('search-screen--is-open')) {
      if (window.DEVICE_VIEW === 'desktop') {
        lockSearchFocus();
      }
      window.TMZ.utils.setAccessibilityFocusTrap('search-screen');
      $search.css('visibility', 'visible');
      setTimeout(function() {
        $nav.css('visibility', 'hidden');
      }, 300);
    } else {
      window.TMZ.utils.removeAccessibilityFocusTrap();
      if (window.DEVICE_VIEW === 'desktop') {
        unlockSearchFocus();
        $mastheadSearchOpenBtn.focus();
      }
      setTimeout(function() {
        $search.css('visibility', 'hidden');
      }, 300);
    }

    // Hide nav
    if ($nav.hasClass('nav--is-open')) {
      setTimeout(function () {
        $nav.removeClass('nav--is-open');
      }, 300);
    }
    event.preventDefault();
  });
});
   </script>

  <script id="newsletter-subscription-success" type="text">
   <p class="thanks">Thank you!<br> You have successfully signed up.</p>
  </script>
  <script>
   wbq.push(function renderSubscribeToNewsletterModal() {
    function renderThankYou() {
      document.getElementById('newsletter-subscription-form').innerHTML = document.getElementById('newsletter-subscription-success').innerHTML;
      window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.destroyComponent('newsletter-subscription-lightbox-root', true));
    }

    function renderComponent(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
      var lightboxDiv = document.createElement('div');
      var lightboxDivId = 'newsletter-subscription-lightbox-root';
      lightboxDiv.setAttribute('id', lightboxDivId);
      document.getElementById('lightbox-root').prepend(lightboxDiv);
      if (window.TMZ.utils.isValidEmail($('#newsletter-subscription-email').val())) {
        window.TMZ.renderComponent(
          'newsletter-subscription-lightbox-root',
          'newsletter-subscription-lightbox',
          {
            email: $('#newsletter-subscription-email').val(),
            id: 'newsletter-subscription-lightbox-root',
          },
        );
        document.addEventListener(window.TMZ.constants.actionTypes.SUBSCRIBE_TO_NEWSLETTER_ACCEPTED, renderThankYou);
      } else {
        alert('Please enter a valid email.');
      }
    }

    $('#newsletter-subscription-form').on('submit', renderComponent);
  });
  </script>
  <div id="ad-adhesion">
  </div>
  <div id="ad-interstitial">
  </div>
  <div id="ad-skin">
  </div>
  <script>
   wbq.push(function renderPage() {
  var isTurbolinksPreview = document.documentElement.hasAttribute('data-turbolinks-preview');
  window.TMZ.dispatch(window.TMZ.actions.renderPage(isTurbolinksPreview));
});
  </script>
 </body>
